### TodoWrite - 2026-01-14 10:15:48 UTC [11:15:48 CEST]

**User Request:** this was the latest implementation - test the mocking and the single-step mode as well as the proper visualization and state management\
All LLM mock infrastructure has been implemented. Here's a summary:

  LLM Mock Mode Implementation

  1. Mock Service (mcp-server-semantic-analysis/src/mock/llm-mock-service.ts)

  Created a comprehensive mock service with:
  - isMockLLMEnabled() - Checks progress file for mock mode flag
  - getMockDelay() - Configurable delay for realistic testing (default 500ms)
  - Mock generators for each agent type:
    - mockSemanticAnalysis() - Context-aware mocks for git/vibe/code analysis
    - mockObservationGeneration() - Mock observations
    - mockInsightGeneration() - Mock insights
    - mockOntologyClassification() - Mock classifications
    - mockQualityAssurance() - Mock QA results
    - mockDeduplicationAnalysis() - Mock dedup results
    - mockStalenessDetection() - Mock staleness detection
    - mockContentValidation() - Mock validation results
    - mockEmbedding() - Deterministic mock embeddings (1536 dimensions)

  2. Coordinator Integration (coordinator.ts)

  - Added mockLLM, mockLLMDelay, mockLLMUpdatedAt to preserved debug state
  - Progress file now persists mock mode across workflow updates

  3. Semantic Analyzer Integration (semantic-analyzer.ts)

  - Added static repositoryPath with setter/getter
  - Mock check in analyzeWithTier() - intercepts all LLM calls when mock mode enabled
  - Metrics tracking for mock calls

  4. Dashboard API (server.js)

  - New endpoint: POST /api/ukb/mock-llm - Enable/disable mock mode
  - Process status includes mockLLM and mockLLMDelay fields

  5. Redux State (ukbSlice.ts)

  - Actions: setMockLLM, syncMockLLMFromServer, resetMockLLMExplicit
